[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn AddressSanitizer-detected stack-buffer-overflow occurs in Wireshark’s ICMP [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissector when running the `handler_icmp` fuzz target. The overflow is triggered in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_icmp_extension` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-icmp.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m via a call to `tvb_memcpy`, which [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39multimately invokes `memcpy` with a write size of [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m bytes that overruns a local [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack buffer. The crash is reproducible under libFuzzer with a small test input.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIssue:[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- During fuzzing of the ICMP dissector [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`handler_icmp`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, AddressSanitizer reports a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“multi-byte-write-stack-buffer-overflow” in the stack frame of [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_icmp_extension` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-icmp.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow happens when `tvb_memcpy` [0m[1;39m([0m[39min tvbuff.c[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m copies [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m bytes into a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocal buffer whose size is smaller, causing writes past the end of that buffer.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mVulnerability type:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Stack-based buffer overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstack-buffer-overflow in memory copying[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mKey observations and findings:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer is invoked with libFuzzer in `interactive` mode, calling [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`handler_icmp` on a single seed corpus file [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for [0m[1;36m100[0m[39m runs.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Sanitizer output pinpoints the overflow to `__asan_memcpy` → `memcpy` → [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_memcpy` at line [0m[1;36m945[0m[39m of tvbuff.c.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The faulty `memcpy` originates in `dissect_interface_identification_object` at [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket-icmp.[0m[1;92mc:927[0m[39m and propagates through `dissect_icmp_extension` at line [0m[1;36m971[0m[39m.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- AddressSanitizer shadow-byte annotations show the overflow begins at stack offset[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m160[0m[39m in the frame of `dissect_icmp_extension`. Several local variables [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`afi.i`, [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`addr_length.i`, `tf_entry.i`, `tf_object`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are partially underflowed by this [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrite.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The crash stack trace also includes higher-level calls through `dissect_icmp`, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`call_dissector_through_handle`, and the fuzz harness entry [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRelevant code areas for further review:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- epan/dissectors/packet-icmp.c, specifically the functions:[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • dissect_interface_identification_object [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m927[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • dissect_icmp_extension [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround lines [0m[1;36m971[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m1092[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • dissect_icmp  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- epan/tvbuff.c, function `tvb_memcpy` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m945[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and overall buffer handling APIs.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The call chain in epan/packet.c that dispatches to the ICMP dissector.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzz harness in wireshark/fuzz/fuzzshark.c, which drives `epan_dissect_run` [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis issue warrants investigation of buffer allocation and length calculations in [0m  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m819[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m820[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mepan/dissectors/packet-icmp.[0m[1;92mc:369[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m379[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m369[0m[39m:#define ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_NAME    [0m[1;36m1[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m370[0m[39m:#define ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_INDEX   [0m[1;36m2[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m371[0m[39m:#define ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_ADDRESS [0m[1;36m3[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m372[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m373[0m[39m:#define ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH  [0m[1;36m128[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m374[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m375[0m[39m:static const value_string ext_echo_ident_str[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[1;39m{[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m376[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m{[0m[39mICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_NAME,    [0m[32m"Identifies Interface By Name"[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m,[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m377[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m{[0m[39mICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_INDEX,   [0m[32m"Identifies Interface By Index"[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m,[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m378[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m{[0m[39mICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_ADDRESS, [0m[32m"Identifies Interface By Address"[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m,[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m379[0m[39m:    [0m[1;39m{[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m, NULL[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mepan/dissectors/packet-icmp.[0m[1;92mc:923[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m933[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m923[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m924[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mswitch[0m[1;39m([0m[39mc_type[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m925[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39mcase ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_NAME:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m926[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Identification Name must be printable*[0m[35m/[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m927[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, ident_name, offset, obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m928[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m929[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mfor [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m930[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mif [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mg_ascii_isprint[0m[1;39m([0m[39mident_name[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m931[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39mbreak;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m932[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m933[0m[39m:    [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mext_object_tree, [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhf_icmp_int_ident_name_string, tvb, offset, obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify the vulnerable code region  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In epan/dissectors/packet-icmp.c, the function [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_interface_identification_object` declares a local stack buffer `uint8_t [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mident_name[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Immediately thereafter, for C-Type `ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_NAME`, the code [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munconditionally does  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, ident_name, offset, obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     without checking that `[0m[1;39m([0m[39mobj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m <= [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m`, causing a [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-buffer-overflow when a malformed packet supplies a larger value.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve existing logic  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The code’s goal is to copy the “identification name” bytes into a temporary [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer for printability checking, and then present them in the protocol tree with [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`proto_tree_add_item`.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must retain the ASCII-printable check [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`g_ascii_isprint`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubsequent call to `proto_tree_add_item` for the same field, but only for the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafely copied/truncated bytes.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch the copy length to prevent overflow  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compute three sizes:  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `raw_len = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mobj_length > [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m : [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;`   [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m The packet-declared [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mname length  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `copy_len = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mraw_len, ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Clamp to buffer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msize  [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • `display_len = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mraw_len, [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;` [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBound by actual TVB data  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Optionally, also clamp `display_len` to `ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH` to ensure[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mGUI won’t attempt to render more bytes than we safely handle.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace the unguarded `tvb_memcpy` with:[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```c[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, ident_name, offset, copy_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Ensure NUL-termination to make future string operations safe[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcopy_len < ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ident_name[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mcopy_len[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[32m'\0'[0m[39m;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Original printable-character check, now only over the safe copy[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       for [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < copy_len; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mg_ascii_isprint[0m[1;39m([0m[39mident_name[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           break;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Display only the validated slice; avoids reading beyond TVB or buffer[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ext_object_tree,[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         hf_icmp_int_ident_name_string,[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         tvb,[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         offset,[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         display_len,[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This ensures the `memcpy` never writes past the [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m-byte stack buffer and the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol tree only attempts to display available bytes.[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Adjust related display length  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The previous code used `obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m` as the length argument to [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`proto_tree_add_item`, which could exceed both the actual TVB remaining length and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe ident_name capacity, causing out-of-bounds reads or confusing display.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By using `display_len`, we restrict the GUI to only valid bytes stored [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mavailable[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the TVB, preventing out-of-range accesses.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Validate the patch  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild Wireshark with AddressSanitizer enabled.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rerun the `handler_icmp` fuzz target with the same seed that triggered the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moriginal crash.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Confirm that the stack-buffer-overflow is no longer reported.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing unit tests and regression tests to ensure this change does not [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbreak normal ICMP extension parsing or user-visible behavior.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Justification and risk mitigation  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This targeted clamp preserves all existing dissection logic: objects still [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshow the same fields, printable-character checks execute as before, and the GUI [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdisplays the same subfield.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We only add bounds checks around the stack buffer, eliminating a critical [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moverflow without altering higher-level parsing or the fuzz harness.  [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Possible side effects: exceptionally long identification names will now be [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtruncated at [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes. In practice, names beyond this length are non-standard and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munlikely to be meaningful; a UI-level notice could be added later if needed.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach matches patterns elsewhere in the ICMP dissector, where object [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlengths are always clamped to local buffer capacities before copying [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., MPLS [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack entries[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
